date: "2018-06-30"

---

We want to formilise in HoTT the intuition behind a correspondance between the
concept of *PathOver* and its respective *total space*. The term PathOver was
briefly mentioned in {% cite hottbook %} and later defined in {% cite Licata2015
%}. It is extensivily used in {%cite hott-in:agda %}.

![](/assets/png-images/2018-07-05-geometry-intution-of-pathovers-7f9fb342.png)

Let's review first an equility type that is closely related with these PathOvers.
(See also {% cite Licata2015 %} for some extra comments).

{: .foldable}

## Homogeneous equality

The *homogeneous equality* is a type `Path` that relate two elements `a₀` and
`a₁` whose types are *definitionally/judgementally. We denote this type as `Path
{A} a₀ a₁`. The curly braces in Agda stands for an *inplicit argument* that the
type-checker infers. We also use the symbol (`_==_`) to denote this type.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1175" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="1181" class="Number">30</a> <a id="1184" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>
<a id="1189" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_==_"></a><a id="1194" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a> <a id="1199" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1200" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1200" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1202" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1204" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1205" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1200" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1216" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1218" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1219" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="1221" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1223" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1205" class="Bound">A</a><a id="1224" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1226" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1205" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1230" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1237" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1200" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1240" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Heterogeneous equality


> In {%cite McBride2004 %} the author introduced a *heterogeneous equality*, which is an equality type
> `a:A= b:B` that relates two elements `a:A` and `b:B` which may have two judgementally
> distinct types, though the reflexivity constructor applies only when both the
> two types and the two terms are judgementally equal.

> However, McBride’s heterogeneous equality is **logically equivalent** to a
> homogeneous equality type *satisfying uniqueness of identity proofs*, which
> is undesirable **in homotopy type theory, because not all types should be sets**.

> This heterogeneous equality relates two elements of two different types along a
> specific equality α between the types. {% cite Licata2015 %}.


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2042" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="HEq₁"></a><a id="2047" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2047" class="Datatype">HEq₁</a> <a   <a id="HEq₁.idp"></a><a id="2132" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2132" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="2136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2138" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2140" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2141" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2141" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="2143" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2145" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2057" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2146" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2148" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2150" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2047" class="Datatype">HEq₁</a> <a id="2155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2057" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2157" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2057" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="2163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2141" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="2165" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#2141" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We adopt the same name `idp` for the reflexivity constructor of the `Path` type
for the heterogeneous equality. This name is convenient because we want to
maintain some consistency in the following proofs. We will switch between
different definitions of heterogeneous equality but also between definitions for
the homogeneous equality.

Let us recall the transport function and the coercion function  along a
homogeneous equality.

  <a id="9838" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="9845" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9845" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="9854" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9855" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9855" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="9858" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9858" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9860" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9862" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9863" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9863" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9865" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9867" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9872" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9855" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="9874" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9876" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9877" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9877" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9879" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9881" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9863" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9883" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9885" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9890" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9858" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9892" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9894" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="9904" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
    <a id="9984" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
    <a id="hott.Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="10026" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10026" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="10035" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10037" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10038" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="10040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10040" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10042" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10044" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10046" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10046" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10048" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9863" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10051" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10053" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10055" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9877" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="10057" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#10046" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10058" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10061" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10063" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="10068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9855" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="10072" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10074" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#9858" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="10076" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="13604" class="Comment">-- Application of an homotopy</a>

    <a id="13707" class="Comment">-- The axiom of function extensionality postulates that the</a>
    <a id="13771" class="Comment">-- application of homotopies is an equivalence.</a>

  <a id="16514" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="16521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16521" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="16534" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="16545" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
    <a id="16616" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
    <a id="hott.Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="16633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16633" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="16640" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16642" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="16644" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16644" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="16645" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="16648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16649" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16649" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16651" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16653" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="16658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16644" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="16659" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16661" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16663" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="16668" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#16644" class="Bound">ℓ</a>

    <a id="23876" class="Comment">-- Half-adjointness implies equivalence.</a>
    <a id="hott.Halfadjoints.ishae-≃"></a><a id="23921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23921" class="Function">ishae-≃</a> <a id="23929" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23931" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23932" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23934" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23936" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#21243" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23938" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23940" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#21257" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23941" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23943" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#21321" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="23951" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#23932" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="23953" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23955" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#21243" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#12516" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="23959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#21257" class="Bound">B</a>

    <a id="26674" class="Comment">-- Quasiinverses create equivalences.</a>

       <a id="28304" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3174" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="28308" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28309" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#27900" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="28316" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28228" class="Bound">α</a><a id="28317" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28319" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3585" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="28321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3174" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="28325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28228" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="28331" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#4348" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="28335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#14024" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="28342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#13322" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="28359" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#28228" class="Bound">α</a><a id="28360" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28362" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#4348" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>

  <a id="28385" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28390" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#27096" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a> <a id="28413" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="28421" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28426" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3037" class="Module">hott</a> <a id="28431" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Let be `α : A == B`, `a : A`, and `b : B` then the following types are equivalent
to the previous type `HEq₁`.

### Equivalences

  <a id="29091" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29091" class="Function">HEq₁-to-HEq₂</a> <a id="29104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29107" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29107" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="29109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29057" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="29113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="29116" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29070" class="Bound">B</a><a id="29117" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="29119" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29119" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="29121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29123" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29057" class="Bound">A</a><a id="29124" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="29126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29126" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="29128" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29130" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#29070" class="Bound">B</a><a id="29131" class="Symbol">}</a>

Finally, we complete the chain of equivalence with `HEq₄-≃-HEq₁`.

{: .foldable}

For the follwing discussion, we may use heterogeneous using the first definition.

## Path over a path

The PathOver is the depedent version of a *path*, what it exactly means is that
we have a path between two endpoints from maybe different types but with. Which
is exactly the same definition of the heterogeneous equality. The difference is
that PathOvers simplifies the `HEq` definition by factorizing the type family
that is involved in the paths.

We first define `PathOver₁` as the inductive family with only one constructor,
the reflexivity over the reflexivity on the base space `A`. To eliminate this
type, we can use path-over induction. In Agda, we just do pattern matching on
the path in the base `A`. We can also define this notion of PathOvers in at least
other four different ways. Let's such definitions all equivalent.

- <pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="33403" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="PathOver₁"></a><a id="33408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33408" class="Datatype">PathOver₁</a> <a id="33418" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33419" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="33422" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33422" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="33424" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33426" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33427" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33429" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33431" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="33435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33419" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="33437" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33440" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33440" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="33442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33427" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33446" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="33453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33422" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="33455" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33457" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33458" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33458" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="33461" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33427" class="Bound">A</a><a id="33464" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33466" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="33474" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33475" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33475" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="33478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33480" - <pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver₅"></a><a id="34278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34278" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="34288" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34290" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="34292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34293" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="34296" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34296" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="34298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34300" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34301" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34303" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34305" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="34310" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34293" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="34312" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="34314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34314" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="34316" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34318" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34301" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34320" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34322" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="34327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34296" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="34329" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34331" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34332" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="34335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34335" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="34338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34340" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34301" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34341" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="34353" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34355" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34356" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="34358" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34332" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="34363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="34366" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34335" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="34368" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34370" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34371" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34374" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34376" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34314" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="34378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34332" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="34380" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="34382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34382" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="34385" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34314" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="34389" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34335" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="34391" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34393" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="34400" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34296" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a>
<a id="34403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34278" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="34413" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34414" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="34416" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34418" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34418" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34419" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34421" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="34427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34427" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34430" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="34433" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34427" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="34438" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="34441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34430" class="Bound">c₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Above when we used `transport C α c₁`, we could also have used `coe (ap C α)`,
both functions are of type `C a₁ → C a₂`. The other case with `c₂` is similar.

### Equivalences

{: .foldable}

    <a id="40067" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="40079" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40079" class="Function">PathOver₅~PathOver₁</a> <a id="40099" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40102" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40102" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="40104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33408" class="Datatype">PathOver₁</a> <a id="40116" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39330" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="40118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="40122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39930" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="40125" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39934" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="40127" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="40139" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40141" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39355" class="Function">PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁</a> <a id="40164" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40165" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39558" class="Function">PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅</a> <a id="40188" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40102" class="Bound">p</a><a id="40189" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="40191" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="40194" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40102" class="Bound">p</a>
      <a id="40202" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40079" class="Function">PathOver₅~PathOver₁</a> <a id="40222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33544" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="40226" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

      <a id="40239" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40239" class="Function">PathOver₁~PathOver₅</a> <a id="40259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40261" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40262" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="40264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40266" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#34278" class="Function">PathOver₅</a> <a id="40276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39330" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="40278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="40282" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39930" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="40285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39934" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="40287" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="40299" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39558" class="Function">PathOver₁-to-PathOver₅</a> <a id="40324" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#39355" class="Function">PathOver₅-to-PathOver₁</a> <a id="40348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40262" class="Bound">p</a><a id="40349" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="40351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="40354" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40262" class="Bound">p</a>
      <a id="40362" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40239" class="Function">PathOver₁~PathOver₅</a> <a id="40382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="40386" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We are going to use the fifth definition for pathovers, the one which is
using an inductive family. Nevertheless, in the following, the reader can change
the subindex of the `PathOver` word to use any other definition.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="40637" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="40646" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40648" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#33842" class="Function">PathOver₃</a>

<a id="40659" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="40665" class="Number">30</a> <a id="40668" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="40677" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="40684" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="40701" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>


> While we have motivated PathOver as a factored heterogeneous equality, there
> is also a geometric intuition. **Dependent types correspond to fibrations**, so a
> type `C : A → Type` can be pictured as its total space `∑ a:A . C` a projecting
> down to `A` by first projection.

> A **path-over** `γ : PathOver C α c­₁ c₂` represents a path σ in `∑ a:A . C` a
> a between `(a₁, c₁)` and `(a₂,c₂)`, such that ap fst σ is exactly `α`. That
> is, it is a path in the total space that projects down to, or lies over, `α`
> (path pairing `pair= α γ` will be made precise below)


## Total spaces

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="41340" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="41347" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41347" class="Module">_</a> <a id="41349" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41350" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41350" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="41353" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41353" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="41355" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41357" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="41359" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41361" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="41366" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41350" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="41368" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41370" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41372" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="41376" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#762" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="41383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41353" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="41385" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41387" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41390" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41390" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="41393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41357" class="Bound">A</a><a id="41396" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41398" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="41407" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41407" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="41418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41420" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41421" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41423" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41425" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41387" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41428" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41390" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41433" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41435" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41438" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41440" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41370" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41442" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41387" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="41444" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41446" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41446" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41451" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41370" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41390" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41455" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="41542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41407" class="Function">Σ-to-==[↓]</a> <a id="41553" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41554" class="Argument">c₁</a> <a id="41557" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41559" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41559" class="Bound">c₁</a><a id="41561" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41564" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="41568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3154" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41570" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="41573" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41575" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41577" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

  <a id="41584" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41584" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="41595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41598" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41387" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41608" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41390" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41610" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41612" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41612" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41617" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41370" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41387" class="Bound">a₁</a><a id="41621" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="41623" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41623" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41626" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41370" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41630" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41390" class="Bound">a₂</a><a id="41632" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="41638" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41641" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41641" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="41643" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41645" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41612" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="41648" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">==</a> <a id="41651" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41623" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="41654" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">[</a> <a id="41656" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41370" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="41658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">↓</a> <a id="41660" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41598" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="41662" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#40637" class="Function">]</a><a id="41663" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="41669" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41671" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3074" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="41673" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="41675" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41387" class="Bound">a₁</a> <a id="41678" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3154" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41612" class="Bound">c₁</a><a id="41682" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41684" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41687" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41390" class="Bound">a₂</a> <a id="41691" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3154" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41693" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41623" class="Bound">c₂</a><a id="41695" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="41698" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="41701" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41701" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="41703" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41706" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#4068" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="41709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3174" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="41713" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41701" class="Bound">q</a><a id="41714" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="41719" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41598" class="Bound">α</a><a id="41720" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="41724" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#41584" class="Function">==[↓]-to-Σ</a> <a id="41735" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41736" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="41739" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41741" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="41745" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41747" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a> <a id="41752" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#3154" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41754" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-pathovers.md %}{% raw %}#1248" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a><a id="41757" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="41762" class="Comment">-- -- more explict:</a>
  <a id="41784" class="Comment">-- ==[↓]-to-Σ {idp}{c₁}{c₂} idp = (idp {a = (a₁ , c₁)}, idp {a = idp {a = a₁}})</a>

  <a id="41867" class="Comment">-- -- Alternative (also type-checked):</a>
  <a id="41908" class="Comment">-- ==[↓]-to-Σ {α = α} γ = (pair= α γ , ap-fst-pair= α γ)</a>
  <a id="41967" class="Comment">--   where</a>
  <a id="41980" class="Comment">--   pair= : ∀ {i j} {A : Type i} {C : A → Type j}</a>
  <a id="42033" class="Comment">--     {a₁ a₂ : A} {c₁ : C a₁} {c₂ : C a₂}</a>
  <a id="42078" class="Comment">--     → (α : a₁ == a₂)</a>
  <a id="42104" class="Comment">--     → (γ : c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ])</a>
  <a id="42140" class="Comment">--     ------</a>
  <a id="42156" class="Comment">--     → (a₁ , c₁) == (a₂ , c₂)</a>
  <a id="42190" class="Comment">--   pair= idp γ = ap (_ ,_) γ</a>
  <a id="42223" class="Comment">--</a>
  <a id="42228" class="Comment">--   ap-fst-pair= : (α : a₁ == a₂)</a>
  <a id="42265" class="Comment">--       → {c₁ : C a₁}{c₂ : C a₂} (γ : c₁ == c₂ [ C ↓ α ] )</a>
  <a id="42327" class="Comment">--       → ap fst (pair= α γ) == α</a>
  <a id="42364" class="Comment">--   ap-fst-pair= idp idp = idp</a>

## Other facts

We can build a dependent path by applying a depedent function to a homogeneous path.
